*********************************************************************************
Commit: 68eb8ef9756a88f0d3d4ecb16140a8e821aa46f5 
*********************************************************************************


  fix UnitTest issue - MicrocodeUpdateFeaturePkg
  
  [Issue Description]
  1. Gcc build error:
  no match function call when setting Return argument to NULL,
  which was due to:
    a. GCC compiler will convert NULL to to long init type
  rather than "VOID *" pointer.
    b. ISO C++ forbids comparison
  between pointer (VOID *) and integer (long int)
  
  2. Gcc build error:
  comparison of integer expression:
  "const long long unsigned int" and "const int" [-Werror=sign-compare]
  
  [Resolution]
  1. Update to use C++ keywords "nullptr"
  of which type was "std::nullptr_t" to declare pointer.
  
  2. Update type casting
  
  Package/Module: MicrocodeUpdateFeaturePkg
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  SererGen3
  
  Hsd-es-id: 15017292414
  
  Change-Id: I4088cf52dd41d4f09ef8f16db72c2b0192fd66de
  Original commit hash: 5dd3d1f33481987e38b3efe892ab2629ab03d487

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 9463c0a326d6f6ea865f68032a6a9b28b970c808 
*********************************************************************************

[PCH]

  Add BIOS support to retrieve MAC address from PSS chip and
  update it into Gbe flash region.
  
  [Feature Description]
  Upon flashing IFWI, MAC address is overwritten with default MAC address
  as 00:00:00:00:00:00. If invalid MAC is written, then platform is not
  able to connect to network.
  
  current solution: Validation system requires overriding of MAC address
  to get the system connected over network. (currently it is done via TTK,
  Dediprog, FPT tool etc).
  
  Need to add BIOS support to retrieve MAC address from PSS chip and
  update it into Gbe flash region.
  
  [Resolution]
  1. Add PssLib as top level functions to read the MAC address from PSS chip.
  2. Port necessary functions from SerialIO to LpssI2c for low-level I2C communications.
          ^^^                                                                            
  3. Add a GbeFwUpdate driver to update the MAC address to Gbe flash region if needed.
  
  Package/Module: GnrwsRpPkg
                  OneSiliconPkg
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  GNRWS.
  
  Hsd-es-id: 15017232823
  
  Change-Id: I6b75dee85dec585e0a233b6302ac16c0bdeef080

Commit: 82dd3f9212979f6a61f2d3807f5f2a7b5b5114f3 
*********************************************************************************


  Invalid assignment of PCIe stacks to Virtual NUMA nodes.
  
  [Issue Description]
  In a 2 sockets system, SNC disabled, Virtual NUMA enabled,
  two virtual nodes were created per socekt, but PCIe in second socket
  is reported in node 1, while 2 is expected.
  
  [Resolution]
  Virtual NUMA was inmplemented by Memory Map like a kind of internal feature.
                                                             ^^^^^^^^          
  The configuration knobs are resolved in effective configuration stored
  in Memory Map HOB. ACPI should use the HOB rather than configuration knobs.
  
  Package/Module:
  ServerPlatformPkg/Acpi
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  All server platforms.
  
  Hsd-es-id: 18040936670

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 8cd762258c4808c1352e00f7487bbd9d0e197153 
*********************************************************************************


  BHS SP 12 way hetero interleaves adjust HpaSize to be spec compliant
                                          ^^                           
  
  [Issue Description]
  CXL HDM decoder size is a value that is not a multiple of 3,
  violating spec, and potentially leaving room for memory address
  access failures in certain edge cases.
  
  [Resolution]
  On BHS SP 12 way interleaves, increase the HpaSize
                                             ^^      
  by 1GB until a multiple of 3 is found.
  
  Package/Module:
  ServerSiliconPkg/MemDecodeLib
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  GNR-SP
  
  Hsd-es-id: 22020575099
  
  Change-Id: If1c5fc253adccb0a886facea56d83a4672b2ae9a
  Original commit hash: f4f6e67b59e486d326e3272a477b7b1dbe66cbd0
  
  [Changed Files]
  ServerSiliconPkg/Mem/Library/MemDecodeLib/Gen3/7nm/MemDecodeCxlNode.c

*********************************************************************************


  Gen4RcdDeviceSupport knob add SETUP_AUTO option as default
  
  [Issue Description]
  Ignoring the Gen4RcdDeviceSupport disable knob for specific configurations
  is confusing and inconsistent with how other knobs are implemented.
        ^^^^^^                                                        
  
  [Resolution]
  Gen4RcdDeviceSupport knob add SETUP_AUTO option as default.
  
  Knob Auto = Function Enabled for GNR-AP, CWF-AP, and CWF-SP. Function Disabled for all others.
  Knob Enable = Function Enabled for all configurations
  Knob Disable = Function Disabled for all configurations

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 81a1fc9537f0e2cab36e6f8011660a1c6f3ad2d7 
*********************************************************************************


  Shall program BcomVref via strap command in JedecInitSequenceSequence()
                             ^^^^^                                        
  
  [Issue Description]
  BcomVref is programmed via strap command at training step. But it is programmed via MRW command at JedecInitSequence.
                             ^^^^^                     ^^^^                                                             
  This results in that: if the default value (75%) after reset is not good enough to send MRW, then may cause some issues.
  
  [Resolution]
  Programmed BcomVref via strap command at JedecInitSequence flow to ensure that BCOM vref can be set to the expected value.
                          ^^^^^                                                                                              
  
  Package/Module:ServerMemoryPkg/BaseDdr5CoreLib
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  GNR, SRF, CWF
  
  Hsd-es-id: 15016850517

  Add PRM Feature Control knob
  
  [Feature Description]
  Add PRM Feature Control knob to enable/disable platform PRM feature.
  By disable this knob, following feature configure will be skipped during boot.
  1. PRM Address Translation (Address Translation will use SMM)
  2. PRM PE Loader
  3. PRM Sample Print
  4. PRM SSDT publish
  
  The PRM feature is enabled by default.

*********************************************************************************


  Corrected frontside TxVref restoring flow in JedecInitSequence().
  
  [Issue Description]
  Db TxVref is restored by PBA mode in RestoreBcom(), which is before PBA enumeration is run.
  The result in that TxVref cannot be set as the expected values at RestoreBcom() step.
                                                                                  ^^^^  
  
  [Resolution]
  1. Set TxVref as the initial values with non-PBA mode at RestoreBcom() to make vref work, which is aligned with the training flow.
  2. Restored the trained values at DoLrBufferInitChannel().
  3. Removed RestoreTxVref() which is called at the end of JedecInitSequence() because TxVref has been restored before (do not need to do this again).
  
  Package/Module:ServerMemoryPkg/BaseDdr5CoreLib
  
  [Impacted Platform]

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 10e045e8916a2f65204ba21115373d69e10ab2d6 
*********************************************************************************


  DisableFastColdBootOnMappedOutRanks function doesn't work
  
  [Issue Description]
  When PcdMrcDisableFastColdBootOnMappedOutRanks is TRUE, it is expected that the function AnyRanksDisabledOrMappedOutMemTestFailures() will disable fast cold boot
  and clear nvram if any ranks or DIMMs have been mapped out due to memory test failures or disable rank calls.
  The function doesn't work due to MemDataGetRankMapOut() being unable to retrieve correct NVRAM values in InitStructures().
  
  [Resolution]
  Move call to AnyRanksDisabledOrMappedOutMemTestFailures() from InitStructures() to inside the memory call table so that NVRAM is updated for all sockets before checking
  if any ranks have been disabled in DetermineBootMode().
  
  Package/Module:
  CpRcPkg/BaseMemoryCoreLib
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  Birch Stream SP
  Birch Stream AP
  Granite Rapids Workstation
  Kaseyville
  Loganville

*********************************************************************************


  [BHS][BKC][BEECHNUT CITY] [SRF SP] [Security][SGX] SGX cannot be enabled by setting MMIO based to 1T/512G on 2DPC Memory config (SgxErrorCode = 0x19)
         ^^                           ^^^^^^^^                                                                                                          
  
  [Issue Description]
  Lowering MMIOH Base down to 512G/1T causes MemDecode to allocate just a
  single PRMRR in a 2S system with 2DPC config.

  distribution check.

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 5821d4c4805b337f5e0f90ab839a20c1f2e7a778 
*********************************************************************************

[PCH]

  Modern standby can't WOL due to PCIe RP MSI.
                                          ^^^  
  
  [Issue Description]
  Modern standby can't wake on LAN due to PCIe RP
  MSI sent with reqID for bus 0 instead of bus M.
  ^^^                                             
  
  [Resolution]
  BIOS required to write all MTL-S PCH PCIe RPs
  mpc.pmme to 0x1, after PCI enumeration,
  and before BIOS DONE, regardless of hot-plug
  capability enabling. In addition to programming
  to enable SMI for PM_PME events.
  
  Package/Module:
  OneSiliconPkg
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  ALL.
  
  Hsd-es-id: 18040118835
  
  Change-Id: I8af61da0979168cb4fb24d4a909656d2eeea8805
  Original commit hash: e18fc20ba7efa5d41a826ce62c16280c88928f85

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 36da13c74bee29677ea2167857750fc2a13a112b 
*********************************************************************************


  Enhanced design for discovering ESP in VROC RAID for seamless recovery
  
  [Issue Description]
  For VROC NVMe RAID configuration, BIOS can't discover ESP in the RAID
  disk to back up files required for seamless recovery. Root cause is that
  the VROC/VMD UEFI driver doesn't fully follow UEFI driver model to
  implement its UEFI driver binding protocol to enumerate all child
  devices behind the RAID controller.
  
  [Resolution]
  Enhance the original design in below aspects:
  1.Follow VROC/VMD UEFI driver design to enumerate all child devices
    behind VMD controller. Some BIOS workarounds are needed to bridge the
                                     ^^^^^^^^^^                           
    gap in design.
  2.Search the ESP in the default order of controller types:
    NVMe > SATA AHCI > VROC NVMe RAID > VROC SATA RAID
  3.Skip re-enumerating child devices behind a controller if they exist
  
  Package/Module: GnrwsRpPkg/Features/CapsuleUpdate/Library/SeamlessRecoverySupportLib
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  GNRWS
  
  Hsd-es-id: 16024933297
  
  Change-Id: I587799405f3933427c7cecfe76fdee40f4f8c4d9
  Original commit hash: a40e81efaa5175bee3148b558fb9db737da461d7
  
  [Changed Files]
  GnrwsRpPkg/Features/CapsuleUpdate/Library/SeamlessRecoverySupportLib/SeamlessRecoverySupportLib.c

*********************************************************************************
Commit: 034c436c9c10c043fb62a8891f4af2f2367688c4 
*********************************************************************************


  [GNR] DRAM CA Vref RMT shall add MR11 as 2nd condition for Pass/Fail criteria
  
  [Issue Description]
  The MPC to set DRAM CaVref may silently fail during a margin sweep. MRC assumes Vref has been updated, but actually the DRAM is in a failed state and the SweepLib should treat the current CaVref setting as a failure.
                                 ^^^^^^                                                                                                                                                                                    
  
  [Resolution]
  The solution is for MRC to perform an MRR of MR11, after the MPC, to confirm if the MPC was successful. If the MRR results doesn't match what MRC things it wrote with the MPC, then the Vref setting is failing.
  
  Besides, MRR command failure is detected during DRAM CA VREF RMT, the trace shows the returned code from MR11 via MRR command, it can be either "valid data on upper or lower with random value" or "invalid data in entire byte".
  Current ReadCpgcMrrData would treat invalid data as error and system would hang, however, it can be just command failure since DRAM CA Vref is swept to boundary of margin. To solve this, MRC shall add command test mode support
  for ReadDramMr API to detect bad command being send during DRAM CA Vref sweep.
  
  Package/Module:
  pRcPkg/Library/BaseDdr5CoreLib
  CpRcPkg/Library/MemSweepLib
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  GNR-SP, CWF-AP, GNR-AP, SRF-AP
  
  Hsd-es-id: 13012260341
  
  Change-Id: I063f11d18275ae844f00ae683bf6f324c1dd50da
  Original commit hash: bdb894123160a587dca4046891246a88d699f24e
  
  [Changed Files]
  CpRcPkg/Include/Library/Ddr5CoreLib.h

  Enable X2APIC for BSP in pre mem phase for specific processor
  
  [Feature Description]
  In MpInitLibInitialize() of PeiMpLib:
  1.MpInitLibInitialize saves the BSP's initial APIC mode and
  syncs to all APs in the first time wakeup in CollectProcessorCount().
  2.If the BSP's Apic mode is LOCAL_APIC_MODE_XAPIC, AutoEnableX2Apic()
  will forcely enable x2APIC mode for both BSP and AP if needed.
  
  Reccently we found that the calling of WakeUpAP in step2 cost a lot of
                                                     ^^^^                
  time on a specific processor. To reduce the time cost of MpInitLibInitialize,
  we can enable X2APIC for BSP in pre mem phase. After that, AP's APIC mode
  will be synced to X2Apic mode during the first call of MpInitLibInitialize
  in CpuMpPei. Then the step2 in MpInitLibInitialize can be skipped.
                        ^^^^                                         
  
  Package/Module:ServerSiliconPkg/Cpu
  
  [Impacted Platform]
  GNR
  
  Hsd-es-id: 15016719938
  
  Change-Id: I9755892574c5d42564bbdbf8f26c16b10cfbdd38
  Original commit hash: ea1fc99b6faecfc8c3e3e44e1cc7be8016cf3d1f
